While visiting friends in Montclair, my wife's Toyota Matrix started leaking under the dash (on her new suede shoes!). We weren't excited about the idea of another breakdown driving from Southern to Northern California, but neither were we excited about going to an unfamiliar mechanic. After research, we found ourselves at Orr Automotive and we're super glad we did.

John treated us right. He walked us through the steps of his diagnosis, took us out to the car to show us his findings, and gave us a discount on additional issues he found 'since he was digging around anyway.' Chris treated us well, too, driving us back to our spot and chatting us up about auto maintenance tips and life in Montclair.

Tl;dr: if you need a diagnosis and solution to a car problem in the Montclair area, go to Orr Automotive. They were kind, knowledgeable, treated us fairly, and acted like they truly wanted to solve our problem affordably and with quality.< /review>

<userid>114998712912984819846<//userid>< Name>
Sukhraj Beasla (Suki)< /Name>
<Date>1409763229958</Date>< rate>
2</rate>
< Text>
The PSL is something I look forward to every holiday season. Starbucks does a good job of debuting this early - online but unfortunately, even after 10 years, their stores manage to royally screw up this experience.

On their PSL specific Twitter account, people were given the opportunity to unlock a code, give the said code to a barista, and get their first PSL. Woohoo! You would think all stores would play along but alas it's always a hassle.

I work near 3 Starbucks locations. The first two I called weren't participating until the next day, the last one I called (this one) said, c'mon by, we'll make it for you with or without the code. Hooray!

I showed up literally 5 minutes later and no one knows what I'm talking about. PSL what? Really? How long have you been around? Do I really need to speak to a manager? Oh, that doesn't start 'til tomorrow. Ugh! I just called you!!

Finally, someone found an email explaining the whole thing, the code, etc. Seriously? Do you not keep up with what your corporate store is doing? Communication royally sucks.

I got my PSL but she did a crappy job of making it. The first PSL of the season is always crappy until they catch on. It's like amateur hour. They really could have been nicer about the whole thing and it would be nice if all stores played along instead of making us all look like fools running around with some mystery code.< /Text>
